    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer6952378645471440448">Since its dedication in 1982, the Vietnam Veterans Memorial has become an American cultural icon symbolizing the war in Vietnam—the defining experience of the Baby Boom generation. The black granite wall of names is one of the most familiar media images associated with the war, and after three decades the memorial remains one of the nation’s most visited monuments.<br/> While t</span>
  <span id="freeText6952378645471440448" style="display:none">Since its dedication in 1982, the Vietnam Veterans Memorial has become an American cultural icon symbolizing the war in Vietnam—the defining experience of the Baby Boom generation. The black granite wall of names is one of the most familiar media images associated with the war, and after three decades the memorial remains one of the nation’s most visited monuments.<br /> While the memorial has enjoyed broad acceptance by the American public, its origins were both humble and contentious. A grassroots effort launched by veterans with no funds, the project was completed in three and a half years. But an emotional debate about aesthetics and the interpretation of heroism, patriotism and history nearly doomed the project. Written from an insider’s perspective, this book tells the complete story of the memorial’s creation amid Washington politics, a nationwide design competition and the heated controversy over the winning design and its creator.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6952378645471440448" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2212229791" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2212229791" />
    <a title="Library Love" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74893905-library-love"><img alt="Library Love" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513106838p2/74893905.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2212229791?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Library Love" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Library Love" href="/user/show/74893905-library-love">Library Love</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2212229791" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6081668061752637875">Personally I have never visited the Vietnam Veterans Memorial (yet, I will do one day) but have long had an interest in this area of our history. Having read certain accounts of the war and the polarizing effect it had on much of our society, I never would have believed equally divisive troubles could have led to such difficulty in erecting the monument, and let’s face it, those brave men and women would suffered through this war deserve at the very least a memorial to their sacrifice. <br/><br/>Doubek ta</span>
  <span id="freeText6081668061752637875" style="display:none">Personally I have never visited the Vietnam Veterans Memorial (yet, I will do one day) but have long had an interest in this area of our history. Having read certain accounts of the war and the polarizing effect it had on much of our society, I never would have believed equally divisive troubles could have led to such difficulty in erecting the monument, and let’s face it, those brave men and women would suffered through this war deserve at the very least a memorial to their sacrifice. <br /><br />Doubek takes an honest journalistic approach here and tries to take perspective from both sides with regard to relevant issues. His book is balanced and unbiased and gives a forthright account of the troubles. This is worth a read for anyone with even a passing interest in history, or governmental procedure in the face of challenge.<br /></span>

<div id="review_1369335365" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1369335365" />
    <a title="Al" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8613162-al"><img alt="Al" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1369335365?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Al" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Al" href="/user/show/8613162-al">Al</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780786479092" href="/book/show/23875579-creating-the-vietnam-veterans-memorial">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1369335365" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17783507592212522017">Excellent book that provides detailed insight into the mechanisms of government bureaucracy when the government attempts to micromanage something.<br/>I met Bob Duoubek in May 2015 at a veteran's meeting on the Holland America Panama Canal Cruise on board the Amsterdam. During the exchange of histories, quite a few involving Vietnam, he mentioned that he had written a book on his experiences while trying to get the Vietnam Veterans Memorial built.<br/>What started as a grass roots effort blew up into an i</span>
  <span id="freeText17783507592212522017" style="display:none">Excellent book that provides detailed insight into the mechanisms of government bureaucracy when the government attempts to micromanage something.<br />I met Bob Duoubek in May 2015 at a veteran's meeting on the Holland America Panama Canal Cruise on board the Amsterdam. During the exchange of histories, quite a few involving Vietnam, he mentioned that he had written a book on his experiences while trying to get the Vietnam Veterans Memorial built.<br />What started as a grass roots effort blew up into an incredibly complex exchange of lies, smoke and mirrors between those who thought they had the right to decide what would be built and politicians and the Vietnam Veterans Memorial Fund organization who took the initial idea and tried to do right by it and the veterans.<br />The story of the infighting and perseverance of the VVMF staff reads better than an action novel. I had to put aside all other reading until I finished this book. And as in any historical account of what happened at a given time for a given action, there are different points of view depending on who you ask. From my reading I believe that Bob Doubek tries to tell the story from all sides and not exaggerate the roles of anyone. If only other accounts of events could be written in a similar manner.<br />Excellent book. Compelling story. Incredible result is the Vietnam Veterans Memorial.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17783507592212522017" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vWfsoXC4oB+MPTvmhljoDWaLBEIBHRR8L45F19LAfOfFnc28rBEShvbXkHew3rH92xYNDMovYIdRndGs5xUPGQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kGLMvbwaVpWsm9ax0F95xFfDAK5ESxFyCLs1xOgQ21/omO2gYLPkDNZxfSDm2SA06l4J4I95ZYl2qKG/3cWooQ==')})
  }

As Chief of Surgical Oncology at Baylor College of Medicine, Dr. Steven Curley has worked with cancer patients for over two decades. While his life\'s work has been to help his patients live longer lives, he found that they helped him in ways he never could have expected. IN MY HANDS is a rare, often emotional look at some of Dr. Curley\'s real patients and real situations in modern cancer care. These stories of resilience, hope, and determination changed and inspired Dr. Curley, and he uses these same stories to encourage patients dealing with the fear and uncertainty coupled with a diagnosis of cancer. Every story in the book has a theme inspired by his patients: Hope, Courage, Strength, Determination, Wonder, Cooperation, Creativity, Diligence, Service, Perseverance, Wisdom, Grace, Consideration, Gratitude, Discernment, Reverence, Resourcefulness, Faith, Beauty, Acceptance, and Empathy. Some are positive messages, reminding us of the importance of maintaining balance between family, work, and leisure activities. Others are examples of the remarkable resilience of the human spirit when facing the reality of and the surgical risks that accompany a cancer diagnosis. Realistically, despite remarkable advances in multidisciplinary cancer care, some remind us cancer is still a potentially lethal and destructive disease affecting patients and the family and friends supporting them. While many people are told that there is no hope in their situation, Dr. Curley\'s patients taught him to always provide hope, to push the envelope and give people a chance, and that hope is a critical component of treatment and care. IN MY HANDS is medical narrative at its finest, and provides insight into medicine and patient care along with fascinating details about one of our most feared diseases.<\/span>\n  <a
